<script>
/* GDPR */
function closeAndAccept() {    
	jQuery('#gdpr-compliance').fadeOut();
    setGDPRCookie();
}

function setGDPRCookie() {
    let date = new Date();
    date.setTime(date.getTime() + (365*24*60*60*1000));
    let expires = "expires=" + date.toGMTString();
    var cookieName = "epilog-gdpr";
    var cookieValue = "true";
    document.cookie = cookieName + "=" + cookieValue + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
}

function getGDPRCookie(gdprCookie) {
  let name = gdprCookie + "=";
  let spli = document.cookie.split(';');	
  for(var j = 0; j < spli.length; j++) {
    let char = spli[j];
    while (char.charAt(0) == ' ') {
      char = char.substring(1);
    }
    if (char.indexOf(name) == 0) {
      return char.substring(name.length, char.length);
    }
  }
  return "";		
}
	
function checkGDPRCookie() {
    if (!getGDPRCookie("epilog-gdpr")) {        
        jQuery('#gdpr').fadeIn();
    }
}

/* Lead and Page Reference Cookies */

var currentURL = window.location.href;
var currentLead = currentURL.replaceAll('_', ' ').split('?=');
var currentReference = currentURL.split('/').filter(e => e).slice(-1);

function setLeadCookie() {
    let date = new Date();
    date.setTime(date.getTime() + (365*24*60*60*1000));
    let expires = "expires=" + date.toGMTString();
	let lead = currentLead[1];
    document.cookie = "epilog-lead=" + lead + ";" + expires + ";path=/";		
}

function setRefCookie() {
    let date = new Date();
    date.setTime(date.getTime() + (365*24*60*60*1000));
    let expires = "expires=" + date.toGMTString();       		
    document.cookie = "epilog-page=" + currentReference + ";" + expires + ";path=/";		
}

function getCookie(epCookie) {
	let name = epCookie + "=";
	let spli = document.cookie.split(';');	
	for(var j = 0; j < spli.length; j++) {
    let char = spli[j];
    while (char.charAt(0) == ' ') {
      char = char.substring(1);
    }
    if (char.indexOf(name) == 0) {
      return char.substring(name.length, char.length);
    }
  }
  return "";		
}
	
function checkCookies() {
	var lead = getCookie("epilog-lead");
	var ref = getCookie("epilog-page");
	// checking whether lead is null or not
	if (lead != "") {
		//if lead is not null then alert
		jQuery('#input_1_25').append(lead);
		jQuery('#input_11_25').append(lead);
		jQuery('#input_13_25').append(lead);
	}	
	if (ref != "") {
		//if ref is not null then alert
		jQuery('#input_1_26').append(ref);
		jQuery('#input_11_26').append(ref);
		jQuery('#input_13_26').append(ref);
	}			
}
	
function checkLead() {		
	if (currentURL.indexOf("?=") > -1){	
		setLeadCookie();		
	}	
	if (jQuery('#gform_1').length) {
		checkCookies();		
	}
	if (jQuery('#gform_11').length) {
		checkCookies();		
	}	
	if (jQuery('#gform_13').length) {
		checkCookies();		
	}	
}

function checkPage(){
	jQuery('a[href$="/kontakt/informationen-anfordern/"]').on('click', function(){
		setRefCookie();		
	});
}

/* Grid Images - Sample Club */

function wrapConsecutiveImages(){
	jQuery(".contentImage").nextAll(".contentImage").addClass('gridImage').after('</div>').prevAll(".contentImage").addClass('gridImage').parent().addClass("gridImagesWrapper");
	jQuery(".gridImagesWrapper br").remove();
}

function convertImages(){
	jQuery('.quickNavContent img, .storyContent img').each(function() {
		var associatedCopy = jQuery(this).parent().prev('p').text();		
		
		jQuery(this).addClass('uk-transition-scale-up uk-transition-opaque').wrap('<a href="' + jQuery(this).attr('src') + '" class="contentImage uk-inline-clip uk-transition-toggle"></a>').after('<div class="uk-transition-fade uk-position-cover uk-overlay-primary"></div><div class="uk-position-center uk-transition-fade"><i class="imgIcon fas fa-search-plus"></i></div>').parent().attr('data-caption', associatedCopy);    
	});
	wrapConsecutiveImages();
}

function setQuickNav(){	
	jQuery('.quickNavContent h2').each(function(i) {
		var stepNum = i + 1;
		var linkName = jQuery(this).attr('id');
		var idName = linkName.replace(/-/g, " ").replace(/_/g, "-");
		jQuery('.quickNavDropdown').append('<li><a href="#' + linkName + '">' + stepNum + '. ' + idName + '</a></li>');		
		jQuery('.quickNavDropdown-lower').append('<li><a href="#' + linkName + '">' + stepNum + '. ' + idName +'</a></li>');
	});					
}

// sets link for multiple product options
function activateBuyButtons(){
	jQuery('.ep-select-switcher').find('option:eq(0)').prop('selected', true);
	jQuery('.ep-select-switcher').change(function(){
		var currentButton = jQuery(this);
		var buyURL = currentButton.children("option:selected").val();
		if( buyURL.length > 0 && buyURL != "" ){
			currentButton.next('.ep-select-switcher-link').attr("href", buyURL).addClass('buy-active');
		}else{
			currentButton.next('.ep-select-switcher-link').attr("href", "").removeClass('buy-active');
		}		
		
	});
}

// Sticky Navbars
UIkit.util.ready(function() {
	UIkit.sticky('.ep-sticky', {offset: 80})
})

// Custom Date formats for international pages
function setIntDateFormat(){
	
	// Check International Current Property
	var CurrentIntProp = document.documentElement.lang;
	// DMY - Europe: AT,AU,BE,CH,CO,DE,DK,ES,FI,FR,ID,IT,LU,MX,NL,NO,PL,PT,RO,UK,
	var dmyArr = ['de-AT','en-AU','fr-BE','de-CH','es-CO','de-DE','da-DK','es-ES','fi-FI','fr-FR','id-ID','it-IT','fr-LU','es-MX','nl','nb-NO','pl-PL','pt-PT','ro-RO','en-GB'];
	// YMD - CN,JP,SE,
	var ymdArr = ['zh-CN','ja-JP','sv-SE'];
	
	jQuery('.int-date').each(function(){		
		var thisDate = jQuery(this);
		var theDate = thisDate.text();
		//a simple date formatting function
		function updateDateFormat(inputDate, format) {
			//parse the input date
			const date = new Date(inputDate);
			//extract the parts of the date
			const day = date.getDate();
			const month = date.getMonth() + 1;
			const year = date.getFullYear();
			//replace the month
			format = format.replace("mm", month.toString().padStart(2,"0"));        
			//replace the year
			if (format.indexOf("yyyy") > -1) {
				format = format.replace("yyyy", year.toString());
			} else if (format.indexOf("yy") > -1) {
				format = format.replace("yy", year.toString().substr(2,2));
			}
			//replace the day
			format = format.replace("dd", day.toString().padStart(2,"0"));
			//return format;
			thisDate.html(format).fadeIn();
		}		
		// DMY
		if (jQuery.inArray(CurrentIntProp,dmyArr) != -1){updateDateFormat(theDate,'dd/mm/yy');}
		// YMD
		else if(jQuery.inArray(CurrentIntProp,ymdArr) != -1) {updateDateFormat(theDate,'yy/mm/dd');}		
		// MDY - US, Canada - Do nothing
		else{thisDate.fadeIn();}
	});
}

jQuery( document ).ready(function() {
	
	if(jQuery('.quickNavContent').length > 0){				
		setQuickNav();		 
		convertImages();
		UIkit.lightbox('.quickNavContent', {toggle: '.contentImage'});
	}
	if(jQuery('.storyContent').length > 0){		
		convertImages();
		UIkit.lightbox('.storyContent', {toggle: '.contentImage'});
	}	
	activateBuyButtons();
	checkLead();
	checkPage();
	checkGDPRCookie();
	
	if( jQuery('.int-date').length ){
		setIntDateFormat();
	}
});
